## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: chemical reaction kinetics
**Analysis**: This task models the rate of change of concentration dA/dt as a function of time t and concentration A. In chemical kinetics, the rate law typically depends on concentration raised to some power (reaction order), and may involve time explicitly for non-elementary or driven reactions.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Zero-order kinetics: dA_dt = c0 (constant rate, independent of concentration)
- First-order kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A (rate proportional to concentration, radioactive decay, simple decomposition)
- Second-order kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A**2 (bimolecular reaction of same species)
- nth-order kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 (general power-law rate dependence)
- Reversible first-order: dA_dt = c0 * A + c1 (first-order with equilibrium/back reaction)
- Mixed order: dA_dt = c0 * A + c1 * A**2 (competing first and second order pathways)
- Michaelis-Menten type: dA_dt = c0 * A / (c1 + A) (enzyme-catalyzed or saturation kinetics)
- Autocatalytic: dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 - A) (logistic-type autocatalytic reaction)
- Inhibition kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A / (c1 + A**2) (substrate inhibition)
- Time-dependent forcing: dA_dt = c0 * A + c1 * t (reaction with linearly varying external input)
- Exponential modulation: dA_dt = c0 * A * exp(c1 * t) (time-dependent rate constant, e.g., temperature ramp)
- Polynomial rate law: dA_dt = c0 + c1 * A + c2 * A**2 + c3 * A**3 (general polynomial in concentration)
- Square root kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A**0.5 (half-order kinetics, surface reactions)
- Cooperative kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 / (c2 + A**c1) (Hill-type cooperative binding/reaction)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Negative rate with positive concentration power → consumption/decay reaction: dA_dt = -c * A^n with c > 0
- Rate independent of A but dependent on t → externally driven or zero-order reaction with time-varying source
- Product of A and (constant - A) → autocatalytic or logistic kinetics where both reactant and product catalyze
- Rational function of A (numerator/denominator both involving A) → enzyme kinetics or surface-catalyzed reactions with adsorption
- Sum of terms with different powers of A → parallel reaction pathways with different molecularities
- Rate proportional to A times a function of t → reaction with time-varying rate constant (e.g., temperature programmed)
- Fractional power of A (e.g., A^0.5) → chain reaction mechanisms or surface-limited heterogeneous catalysis
- Quadratic or cubic terms in A appearing with alternating signs → complex reaction networks with competing formation and consumption
